2. It consists of two terms: a quadratic term $c_0 A^2$ and a rational term $\frac{c_2 A^2}{c_4 A^4 + 1}$.
3. The rational term has the form $\frac{A^2}{A^4 + \text{const}}$.

For any candidate to match, all t-dependent terms must be eliminable (set to zero), and the remaining A-dependent structure must be algebraically equivalent.

Let me analyze each candidate:

### Candidate 1: $A^2 c_0 + \frac{A^{c_1} c_2}{A^{c_1} + c_3} + c_4 + c_5 \exp(c_6 t) + c_7 \exp(c_8 t) \log(c_9|A|+1)$

Set $c_5=0, c_7=0, c_4=0$. Remaining: $A^2 c_0 + \frac{A^{c_1} c_2}{A^{c_1} + c_3}$.

GT's rational part is $\frac{0.45987 A^2}{0.74980 A^4 + 1}$. Can $\frac{A^{c_1} c_2}{A^{c_1} + c_3}$ match this?

Setting $c_1 = 2$: $\frac{c_2 A^2}{A^2 + c_3}$. This has denominator $A^2 + c_3$, but GT has $A^4 + \text{const}$ in denominator. These are different rational functions — NOT equivalent.

Setting $c_1 = 4$: $\frac{c_2 A^4}{A^4 + c_3}$. This is $A^4/(A^4+c_3)$ type, not $A^2/(A^4+c_3)$. NOT equivalent.

No value of $c_1$ works because we need $A^2$ in numerator and $A^4$ in denominator simultaneously.

Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 2: $A^2(c_0+c_1) + A(c_2+c_3) + A c_4 \log(c_5|A|+1) + A c_6 \exp(c_7 t) + c_8 t \exp(c_9 t)$

Set $c_6=0, c_8=0$. Remaining: $A^2 \cdot \text{const} + A \cdot \text{const} + A c_4 \log(c_5|A|+1)$.

This has $A \log(|A|+\text{const})$ which cannot produce a rational function $A^2/(A^4+1)$. 

Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 3: $A^2 c_0 + Ac_1 + Ac_2 \max(0, c_3 t + c_4) + Ac_5 \exp(c_6 t) + c_7 t \exp(c_8 t)$

Set $c_5=0, c_7=0$, and set $c_2=0$ or $c_4$ large enough. Remaining: $A^2 c_0 + A c_1$. This is polynomial, cannot match the rational term.

Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 4: $A^2 c_0 + c_1 + c_2/|A|^5$

No rational term of the right form. $1/A^5$ is not equivalent to $A^2/(A^4+1)$.

Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 5: $A^2 c_0 + Ac_1 + Ac_2 \max(0, c_3 t + c_4) + \frac{A^{c_5} c_6}{A^{c_5} + c_7} + c_8 t \exp(c_9 t)$

Set $c_1=0, c_2=0, c_8=0$. Remaining: $A^2 c_0 + \frac{A^{c_5} c_6}{A^{c_5} + c_7}$.

Same issue as Candidate 1. Need $A^2/(A^4+\text{const})$. With $c_5=2$: $A^2/(A^2+c_7)$ — wrong. With $c_5=4$: $A^4/(A^4+c_7)$ — wrong numerator power.

Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 6: $A^2 c_0 + Ac_1 + Ac_2 \exp(c_3 t) + \frac{Ac_4}{A+c_5} + Ac_6 + c_7 \exp(c_3 t)$

Set $c_2=0, c_7=0$. Remaining: $A^2 c_0 + A(c_1+c_6) + \frac{Ac_4}{A+c_5}$.

$\frac{A}{A+c_5}$ is a different rational structure than $\frac{A^2}{A^4+1}$.

Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 7: $A^2 c_0 + \frac{Ac_1}{A+c_2} + Ac_3 + \frac{Ac_4}{c_5 t+1} + \frac{c_6 t}{c_7+t^2}$

Set $c_4=0, c_6=0$. Remaining: $A^2 c_0 + Ac_3 + \frac{Ac_1}{A+c_2}$. Wrong rational structure.

Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 8: $\frac{A^2 c_0 t}{c_1+t} + \frac{A^2 c_2}{c_1+t} + \frac{A^{c_3} c_4}{A^{c_3}+c_5} + \frac{c_6 t}{c_1+t}$

The first, second, and fourth terms combine: $\frac{A^2 c_0 t + A^2 c_2 + c_6 t}{c_1+t}$.

For t-independence of the $A^2$ part: $\frac{A^2(c_0 t + c_2)}{c_1+t}$. For this to be t-independent, we need $c_0 t + c_2 = k(c_1+t)$, so $c_0 = k$ and $c_2 = k c_1$. Then this becomes $k A^2$.

The $\frac{c_6 t}{c_1+t}$ term is t-dependent and can only be eliminated by $c_6=0$.

So remaining: $kA^2 + \frac{A^{c_3} c_4}{A^{c_3}+c_5}$.

Same issue as before — $\frac{A^{c_3}}{A^{c_3}+c_5}$ can't match $\frac{A^2}{A^4+1}$.

Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 9: $Ac_0 + c_1 + \frac{c_2 \exp(c_3 t)}{|A|^5} + c_4 \sin(c_5 \log(c_6|A|+1)+c_7) + \frac{c_8}{A^5}$

Wrong basis functions entirely.

Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 10: $A^2 c_0 + A^{c_1} c_2 + c_3 \exp(Ac_4) \log(c_5 t+1)$

Set $c_3=0$. Remaining: $A^2 c_0 + A^{c_1} c_2$. This is a sum of power functions, not a rational function.

Candidate 10 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 11: $A^2(c_0+c_1+c_2) + A(c_3+c_4) + \frac{Ac_5 \exp(c_6 t)}{A+c_7} + c_8 t \exp(c_9 t)$

Set $c_5=0, c_8=0$. Remaining: polynomial in A. Can't match rational term.

Candidate 11 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 12: $A^2 c_0 + Ac_1 + Ac_2 + c_3 + c_4 t \exp(c_5 t) + (c_6|A|+1)^{-5}$

Set $c_4=0$. Remaining: $A^2 c_0 + A(c_1+c_2) + c_3 + (c_6|A|+1)^{-5}$.

$(c_6 A+1)^{-5}$ is not the same form as $A^2/(A^4+1)$.

Candidate 12 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 13: $\frac{A^2 c_0 t}{c_1+t} + A^2 c_2 + \frac{A^2 c_3}{c_1+t} + Ac_4 + \frac{c_5 t}{c_1+t}$

Set $c_4=0, c_5=0$. Remaining: $A^2 c_2 + \frac{A^2(c_0 t + c_3)}{c_1+t}$.

This simplifies to $A^2[c_2 + \frac{c_0 t + c_3}{c_1+t}]$. This is just $A^2 \cdot f(t)$, which is t-dependent unless we make it constant. Even then, it's just $\text{const} \cdot A^2$. Can't produce the rational term.

Candidate 13 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 14: $A^2 c_0 + \frac{A^{c_1} c_2}{A^{c_1}+c_3} + c_4 + c_5 \exp(c_6 t)$

Set $c_4=0, c_5=0$. Same as Candidate 1's core: $A^2 c_0 + \frac{A^{c_1} c_2}{A^{c_1}+c_3}$. Can't match.

Candidate 14 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 15: $A^2 c_0 + \frac{Ac_1}{Ac_2+c_3} + Ac_4$

Set $c_4=0$. $A^2 c_0 + \frac{Ac_1}{Ac_2+c_3}$. The rational part is $\frac{A}{A+\text{const}}$ type. Not matching $\frac{A^2}{A^4+1}$.

Candidate 15 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 16: $\frac{A^{2+c_0} c_1}{A^{c_0}+c_2} + \frac{A^2 c_3}{A^{c_0}+c_2} + \frac{Ac_4 \exp(c_5 t)}{1} + \frac{A^{c_0} c_6}{A^{c_0}+c_2}$

Wait, let me re-read: $\frac{A^2 \cdot A^{c_0} \cdot c_1}{A^{c_0}+c_2} + \frac{A^2 c_3}{A^{c_0}+c_2} + Ac_4 \exp(c_5 t) + \frac{A^{c_0} c_6}{A^{c_0}+c_2}$

Set $c_4=0$. Combine over common denominator $A^{c_0}+c_2$:

$\frac{A^{2+c_0} c_1 + A^2 c_3 + A^{c_0} c_6}{A^{c_0}+c_2}$

Set $c_0=4$: $\frac{A^6 c_1 + A^2 c_3 + A^4 c_6}{A^4+c_2}$

GT is $-0.19 A^2 + \frac{0.46 A^2}{0.75 A^4+1} = \frac{-0.19 A^2(0.75 A^4+1) + 0.46 A^2}{0.75 A^4+1} = \frac{-0.1425 A^6 + 0.27 A^2}{0.75 A^4+1}$

So GT = $\frac{-0.1425 A^6 + 0.27 A^2}{0.75 A^4+1}$

Candidate 16 with $c_0=4$: $\frac{c_1 A^6 + c_6 A^4 + c_3 A^2}{A^4+c_2}$

GT has no $A^4$ term in numerator. Set $c_6=0$: $\frac{c_1 A^6 + c_3 A^2}{A^4+c_2}$

This matches the GT structure! Set $c_2 = 1/0.75 = 4/3$, $c_1 = -0.1425/1 \cdot (1/0.75)$... Let me be more careful.

GT = $\frac{-0.1425 A^6 + 0.27 A^2}{0.75 A^4+1}$

Candidate: $\frac{c_1 A^6 + c_3 A^2}{A^4+c_2}$

We can multiply GT numerator and denominator by $1/0.75$: $\frac{-0.19 A^6 + 0.36 A^2}{A^4 + 1.333}$

So $c_1 = -0.19$, $c_3 = 0.36$, $c_2 = 1.333$. Let me verify:

$-0.18998 \times 0.74980 = -0.14245$. And $0.45987/0.74980 \times 0.74980 = 0.45987$... 

Let me recompute GT numerator: $-0.18998 \cdot 0.74980 \cdot A^6 - 0.18998 \cdot A^2 + 0.45987 \cdot A^2 = -0.14243 A^6 + 0.26989 A^2$

Candidate: $\frac{c_1 A^6 + c_3 A^2}{A^4 + c_2}$. Set $c_2 = 1/0.74980$, $c_1 = -0.14243/1 \cdot 0.74980 = -0.18998/1$... 

Actually, to match: $\frac{c_1 A^6 + c_3 A^2}{A^4+c_2} = \frac{(-0.14243 A^6 + 0.26989 A^2)/0.74980}{(0.74980 A^4+1)/0.74980} = \frac{-0.14243 A^6 + 0.26989 A^2}{0.74980 A^4+1}$

Wait, that doesn't work because dividing numerator and denominator by 0.74980:

$\frac{-0.14243 A^6 + 0.26989 A^2}{0.74980 A^4+1} = \frac{(-0.14243/0.74980) A^6 + (0.26989/0.74980) A^2}{A^4+1/0.74980}$

$= \frac{-0.18998 A^6 + 0.35996 A^2}{A^4 + 1.33369}$

So $c_1 = -0.18998$, $c_3 = 0.35996$, $c_2 = 1.33369$, $c_0 = 4$, $c_4 = 0$, $c_6 = 0$.

This works! ✓

Candidate 16 verdict: [MATCH]

### Candidate 17: $A^2 c_0 + Ac_1 \exp(c_2 t) + A^{c_3} c_4$

Set $c_1=0$. Remaining: $A^2 c_0 + A^{c_3} c_4$. Power functions only, no rational term.

Candidate 17 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 18: $\frac{A^2 c_0 t}{c_1+t} + \frac{A^2 c_2}{c_1+t} + \frac{Ac_3}{Ac_4+1} + \frac{Ac_5}{A+c_6} + \frac{c_7 t}{c_1+t}$

Set $c_7=0$. The $A^2$ terms: $\frac{A^2(c_0 t + c_2)}{c_1+t}$. Make t-independent: $c_0 = k, c_2 = kc_1$, giving $kA^2$.

Remaining rational terms: $\frac{Ac_3}{Ac_4+1} + \frac{Ac_5}{A+c_6}$. These are $\frac{A}{A+\text{const}}$ type terms. Can two such terms combine to give $\frac{A^2}{A^4+\text{const}}$? 

$\frac{Ac_3}{Ac_4+1} + \frac{Ac_5}{A+c_6}$. Common denominator: $(Ac_4+1)(A+c_6)$. Numerator: $Ac_3(A+c_6) + Ac_5(Ac_4+1) = A^2(c_3+c_4 c_5) + A(c_3 c_6 + c_5)$.

Denominator: $c_4 A^2 + (c_4 c_6+1)A + c_6$.

This is a ratio of degree-2 polynomial over degree-2 polynomial. GT's rational part is $\frac{A^2}{A^4+\text{const}}$, degree 2 over degree 4. Can't match.

Candidate 18 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 19: Complex expression with many terms. Let me check if it can produce the right structure.

$\frac{A^{c_0} c_1 t}{c_2+t} + \frac{A^{c_0} c_3}{c_2+t} + A^{c_4} c_5 + \frac{c_6 \exp(Ac_7)}{c_2+t} + \frac{c_8 t}{c_2+t} + \frac{c_9 t \exp(Ac_7)}{c_2+t}$

This has exponential terms in A ($\exp(Ac_7)$), which can't match rational functions unless set to zero. Set $c_6=0, c_9=0$. Also set $c_8=0$.

Remaining: $\frac{A^{c_0}(c_1 t + c_3)}{c_2+t} + A^{c_4} c_5$

Make first term t-independent: $c_1 = k, c_3 = kc_2$, giving $kA^{c_0}$.

So: $kA^{c_0} + c_5 A^{c_4}$. Just power functions. Can't match.

Candidate 19 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 20: $A^2 c_0 + Ac_1 + c_2 + \frac{c_3 \exp(c_4 t)}{|A|^5} + \frac{c_5}{A^5}$

Set $c_3=0$. Remaining has $1/A^5$ which is wrong structure.

Candidate 20 verdict: [NO MATCH]

Candidate 23 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 24: $\frac{A^2 c_0 t}{c_1+t} + \frac{A^2 c_2}{c_1+t} + Ac_3 + \frac{Ac_4}{A+c_5} + \frac{c_6 t}{c_1+t}$

### Candidate 26: $A^2 c_0 + A^2 c_1 \exp(c_2 t) + A^{c_3} c_4 + c_5 \log(c_6 \exp(A^{c_7} c_8)+1)$

Set $c_1=0$. Remaining: $A^2 c_0 + A^{c_3} c_4 + c_5 \log(c_6 \exp(A^{c_7} c_8)+1)$.

The log-exp term: if $c_6 \exp(A^{c_7} c_8) \gg 1$, it approximates $A^{c_7} c_8 + \log c_6$, but we can't use approximations. This is a softplus-like function, not a rational function.

Candidate 26 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 27: $A^2(c_0+c_1) + A(c_2+c_4) + \frac{Ac_2}{A+c_3} + \frac{Ac_5}{Ac_6+1} + c_7 + c_8 \exp(c_9 t)$

Wait, let me re-read: $A^2 c_0 + A^2 c_1 + Ac_2 + Ac_3 + \frac{Ac_2}{A+c_3}$... No, it's:

$A^2 c_0 + A^2 c_1 + \frac{Ac_2}{A+c_3} + Ac_4 + \frac{Ac_5}{Ac_6+1} + c_7 + c_8 \exp(c_9 t)$

Set $c_4=0, c_7=0, c_8=0$. Remaining: $A^2(c_0+c_1) + \frac{Ac_2}{A+c_3} + \frac{Ac_5}{Ac_6+1}$.

Two rational terms of $\frac{A}{A+\text{const}}$ type. Their sum has degree-2/degree-2 rational part. Can't match degree-2/degree-4.

Candidate 27 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 28: $c_0 t \exp(c_1 t) + c_2 + c_3 \exp(c_4|A|) + c_5|A|^{c_6}$

Candidate 28 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 29: $\frac{A^2 c_0 t}{c_1+t} + \frac{A^2 c_2}{c_1+t} + \frac{c_3 t}{c_1+t} + c_4 \log(c_5 \exp(Ac_6)+1)$

### Candidate 30: $A^2 c_0 + Ac_1 \exp(c_2 t) + Ac_3 + A^{c_4} c_5 \log(Ac_6+1) + \frac{c_7 t}{c_8+t^2}$

Candidate 30 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 31: $\frac{A^2 c_2}{A+c_1} + \frac{Ac_3}{A+c_1} + \frac{Ac_4 \exp(c_5 t)|A|^{c_6}}{A+c_1} + \frac{c_7 \exp(c_5 t)|A|^{c_6}}{A+c_1}$

Wait: $\frac{A^2 c_0}{A+c_1} + \frac{Ac_2}{A+c_1} + \frac{Ac_3}{A+c_1} + \frac{Ac_4 \exp(c_5 t)|A|^{c_6}}{A+c_1} + \frac{c_7 \exp(c_5 t)|A|^{c_6}}{A+c_1}$

Set $c_4=0, c_7=0$. Remaining: $\frac{A^2 c_0 + A(c_2+c_3)}{A+c_1}$.

This is a degree-2/degree-1 rational function. By polynomial division: $c_0 A + (c_2+c_3-c_0 c_1) + \frac{c_1(c_0 c_1 - c_2 - c_3)}{A+c_1}$. This can't match $A^2/(A^4+1)$.

Candidate 31 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 32: $Ac_0 + c_1 t \exp(c_2 t) + c_3 + c_4/|A|^5$

Set $c_1=0$. Remaining: $Ac_0 + c_3 + c_4/|A|^5$. Wrong structure.

Candidate 32 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 33: $Ac_0 \exp(c_1 t) + c_2 t \exp(c_3 t) + c_4|A| + c_5$

Set $c_0=0, c_2=0$. Remaining: $c_4 A + c_5$ (using $A \geq 0$). Linear, not matching.

Candidate 33 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 34: $\frac{A^3 c_0 + A^2 c_2 + A \cdot A^{c_3} c_4 + Ac_5 + A^{c_3} c_6}{A+c_1}$

This is a rational function with denominator $A+c_1$ (degree 1). The GT has denominator of degree 4. Can't match unless the expression simplifies, but degree-1 denominator can't produce degree-4 denominator behavior.

Actually wait — could the whole expression be polynomial? If $c_1=0$, denominator is $A$, and we get: $A^2 c_0 + Ac_2 + A^{c_3} c_4 + c_5 + A^{c_3-1} c_6$. Still power functions.
